get_specials(self) -\u0026gt; Annotated[str, \u0026quot;Returns the specials from the menu.\u0026quot;]:\n        return \u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\n        Special Soup: Clam Chowder\n <p dir="auto"><strong>Build intelligent AI agents and multi-agent systems with this enterprise-ready orchestration framework</strong></p>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/microsoft/semantic-kernel/blob/main/LICENSE"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/8a32dcb5cfce2f81c84f36af9a479c82f4779bc89950e62cbd05b4afe95a2377/68747470733a2f2f696d672e736869656c64732e696f2f6769746875622f6c6963656e73652f6d6963726f736f66742f73656d616e7469632d6b65726e656c" alt="License: MIT" data-canonical-src="https://img.shields.io/github/license/microsoft/semantic-kernel" style="max-width: 100%;"></a>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">What is Semantic Kernel?</h2><a id="user-content-what-is-semantic-kernel" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: What is Semantic Kernel?" href="#what-is-semantic-kernel"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Semantic Kernel is a model-agnostic SDK that empowers developers to build, orchestrate, and deploy AI agents and multi-agent systems. Whether you're building a simple chatbot or a complex multi-agent workflow, Semantic Kernel provides the tools you need with enterprise-grade reliability and flexibility.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">System Requirements</h2><a id="user-content-system-requirements" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: System Requirements" href="#system-requirements"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Python</strong>: 3.10+</li>
<li><strong>.NET</strong>: .NET 10.0+</li>
<li><strong>Java</strong>: JDK 17+</li>
<li><strong>OS Support</strong>: Windows, macOS, Linux</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Key Features</h2><a id="user-content-key-features" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Key Features" href="#key-features"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Model Flexibility</strong>: Connect to any LLM with built-in support for <a href="https://platform.openai.com/docs/introduction" rel="nofollow">OpenAI</a>, <a href="https://azure.microsoft.com/en-us/products/ai-services/openai-service" rel="nofollow">Azure OpenAI</a>, <a href="https://huggingface.co/" rel="nofollow">Hugging Face</a>, <a href="https://www.nvidia.com/en-us/ai-data-science/products/nim-microservices/" rel="nofollow">NVidia</a> and more</li>
<li><strong>Agent Framework</strong>: Build modular AI agents with access to tools/plugins, memory, and planning capabilities</li>
<li><strong>Multi-Agent Systems</strong>: Orchestrate complex workflows with collaborating specialist agents</li>
<li><strong>Plugin Ecosystem</strong>: Extend with native code functions, prompt templates, OpenAPI specs, or Model Context Protocol (MCP)</li>
<li><strong>Vector DB Support</strong>: Seamless integration with <a href="https://learn.microsoft.com/en-us/azure/search/search-what-is-azure-search" rel="nofollow">Azure AI Search</a>, <a href="https://www.elastic.co/" rel="nofollow">Elasticsearch</a>, <a href="https://docs.trychroma.com/getting-started" rel="nofollow">Chroma</a>, and more</li>
<li><strong>Multimodal Support</strong>: Process text, vision, and audio inputs</li>
<li><strong>Local Deployment</strong>: Run with <a href="https://ollama.com/" rel="nofollow">Ollama</a>, <a href="https://lmstudio.ai/" rel="nofollow">LMStudio</a>, or <a href="https://onnx.ai/" rel="nofollow">ONNX</a></li>
<li><strong>Process Framework</strong>: Model complex business processes with a structured workflow approach</li>
<li><strong>Enterprise Ready</strong>: Built for observability, security, and stable APIs</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Installation</h2><a id="user-content-installation" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Installation" href="#installation"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Basic Agent - Python</h3><a id="user-content-basic-agent---python" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Basic Agent - Python" href="#basic-agent---python"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Create a simple assistant that responds to user prompts:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="import asyncio
from semantic_kernel.agents import ChatCompletionAgent
from semantic_kernel.connectors.ai.open_ai import AzureChatCompletion

async def main():
    # Initialize a chat agent with basic instructions
    agent = ChatCompletionAgent(
        service=AzureChatCompletion(),
        name=&quot;SK-Assistant&quot;,
        instructions=&quot;You are a helpful assistant.&quot;,
    )

    # Get a response to a user message
    response = await agent.get_response(messages=&quot;Write a haiku about Semantic Kernel.&quot;)
    print(response.content)

asyncio.run(main()) 

# Output:
# Language's essence,
# Semantic threads intertwine,
# Meaning's core revealed."><pre><span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">asyncio</span>
<span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s1">semantic_kernel</span>.<span class="pl-s1">agents</span> <span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-v">ChatCompletionAgent</span>
<span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s1">semantic_kernel</span>.<span class="pl-s1">connectors</span>.<span class="pl-s1">ai</span>.<span class="pl-s1">open_ai</span> <span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-v">AzureChatCompletion</span>

<span class="pl-k">async</span> <span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>():
    <span class="pl-c"># Initialize a chat agent with basic instructions</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">agent</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">ChatCompletionAgent</span>(
        <span class="pl-s1">service</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-en">AzureChatCompletion</span>(),
        <span class="pl-s1">name</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"SK-Assistant"</span>,
        <span class="pl-s1">instructions</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"You are a helpful assistant."</span>,
    )

    <span class="pl-c"># Get a response to a user message</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">response</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">await</span> <span class="pl-s1">agent</span>.<span class="pl-c1">get_response</span>(<span class="pl-s1">messages</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"Write a haiku about Semantic Kernel."</span>)
    <span class="pl-en">print</span>(<span class="pl-s1">response</span>.<span class="pl-c1">content</span>)

<span class="pl-c"># Output:</span>
<span class="pl-c"># Language's essence,</span>

<div class="highlight highlight-source-cs notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="using Microsoft.SemanticKernel;
using Microsoft.SemanticKernel.Agents;

var builder = Kernel.CreateBuilder();
builder.AddAzureOpenAIChatCompletion(
                Environment.GetEnvironmentVariable(&quot;AZURE_OPENAI_DEPLOYMENT&quot;),
                Environment.GetEnvironmentVariable(&quot;AZURE_OPENAI_ENDPOINT&quot;),
                Environment.GetEnvironmentVariable(&quot;AZURE_OPENAI_API_KEY&quot;)
                );
var kernel = builder.Build();

ChatCompletionAgent agent =
    new()
    {
        Name = &quot;SK-Agent&quot;,
        Instructions = &quot;You are a helpful assistant.&quot;,
        Kernel = kernel,
    };

await foreach (AgentResponseItem&lt;ChatMessageContent&gt; response 
    in agent.InvokeAsync(&quot;Write a haiku about Semantic Kernel.&quot;))
{
    Console.WriteLine(response.Message);
}

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Agent with Plugins - Python</h3><a id="user-content-agent-with-plugins---python" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Agent with Plugins - Python" href="#agent-with-plugins---python"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Enhance your agent with custom tools (plugins) and structured output:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="import asyncio
from typing import Annotated
from pydantic import BaseModel
from semantic_kernel.agents import ChatCompletionAgent
from semantic_kernel.connectors.ai.open_ai import AzureChatCompletion, OpenAIChatPromptExecutionSettings
from semantic_kernel.functions import kernel_function, KernelArguments

class MenuPlugin:
    @kernel_function(description=&quot;Provides a list of specials from the menu.&quot;)
    def get_specials(self) -&gt; Annotated[str, &quot;Returns the specials from the menu.&quot;]:
        return &quot;&quot;&quot;
        Special Soup: Clam Chowder
        Special Salad: Cobb Salad
        Special Drink: Chai Tea
        &quot;&quot;&quot;

    @kernel_function(description=&quot;Provides the price of the requested menu item.&quot;)
    def get_item_price(
        self, menu_item: Annotated[str, &quot;The name of the menu item.&quot;]
    ) -&gt; Annotated[str, &quot;Returns the price of the menu item.&quot;]:
        return &quot;$9.99&quot;

class MenuItem(BaseModel):
    price: float
    name: str

async def main():
    # Configure structured output format
    settings = OpenAIChatPromptExecutionSettings()
    settings.response_format = MenuItem

    # Create agent with plugin and settings
    agent = ChatCompletionAgent(
        service=AzureChatCompletion(),
        name=&quot;SK-Assistant&quot;,
        instructions=&quot;You are a helpful assistant.&quot;,
        plugins=[MenuPlugin()],
        arguments=KernelArguments(settings)
    )

    response = await agent.get_response(messages=&quot;What is the price of the soup special?&quot;)
    print(response.content)

    # Output:
    # The price of the Clam Chowder, which is the soup special, is $9.99.

asyncio.run(main()) "><pre><span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">asyncio</span>
<span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s1">typing</span> <span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-v">Annotated</span>
<span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s1">pydantic</span> <span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-v">BaseModel</span>
<span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s1">semantic_kernel</span>.<span class="pl-s1">agents</span> <span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-v">ChatCompletionAgent</span>
<span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s1">semantic_kernel</span>.<span class="pl-s1">connectors</span>.<span class="pl-s1">ai</span>.<span class="pl-s1">open_ai</span> <span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-v">AzureChatCompletion</span>, <span class="pl-v">OpenAIChatPromptExecutionSettings</span>
<span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s1">semantic_kernel</span>.<span class="pl-s1">functions</span> <span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">kernel_function</span>, <span class="pl-v">KernelArguments</span>

<span class="pl-k">class</span> <span class="pl-v">MenuPlugin</span>:
    <span class="pl-en">@<span class="pl-en">kernel_function</span>(<span class="pl-s1">description</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"Provides a list of specials from the menu."</span>)</span>
    <span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">get_specials</span>(<span class="pl-s1">self</span>) <span class="pl-c1">-&gt;</span> <span class="pl-v">Annotated</span>[<span class="pl-smi">str</span>, <span class="pl-s">"Returns the specials from the menu."</span>]:
        <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s">"""</span>
<span class="pl-s">        Special Soup: Clam Chowder</span>
<span class="pl-s">        Special Salad: Cobb Salad</span>
<span class="pl-s">        Special Drink: Chai Tea</span>
<span class="pl-s">        """</span>

    <span class="pl-en">@<span class="pl-en">kernel_function</span>(<span class="pl-s1">description</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"Provides the price of the requested menu item."</span>)</span>
    <span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">get_item_price</span>(
        <span class="pl-s1">self</span>, <span class="pl-s1">menu_item</span>: <span class="pl-v">Annotated</span>[<span class="pl-smi">str</span>, <span class="pl-s">"The name of the menu item."</span>]
    ) <span class="pl-c1">-&gt;</span> <span class="pl-v">Annotated</span>[<span class="pl-smi">str</span>, <span class="pl-s">"Returns the price of the menu item."</span>]:
        <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s">"$9.99"</span>

<span class="pl-k">class</span> <span class="pl-v">MenuItem</span>(<span class="pl-v">BaseModel</span>):
    <span class="pl-s1">price</span>: <span class="pl-smi">float</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">name</span>: <span class="pl-smi">str</span>

<span class="pl-k">async</span> <span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>():
    <span class="pl-c"># Configure structured output format</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">settings</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">OpenAIChatPromptExecutionSettings</span>()
    <span class="pl-s1">settings</span>.<span class="pl-c1">response_format</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-v">MenuItem</span>

    <span class="pl-c"># Create agent with plugin and settings</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">agent</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">ChatCompletionAgent</span>(
        <span class="pl-s1">service</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-en">AzureChatCompletion</span>(),
        <span class="pl-s1">name</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"SK-Assistant"</span>,
        <span class="pl-s1">instructions</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"You are a helpful assistant."</span>,
        <span class="pl-s1">plugins</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span>[<span class="pl-en">MenuPlugin</span>()],
        <span class="pl-s1">arguments</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-en">KernelArguments</span>(<span class="pl-s1">settings</span>)
    )

    <span class="pl-s1">response</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">await</span> <span class="pl-s1">agent</span>.<span class="pl-c1">get_response</span>(<span class="pl-s1">messages</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"What is the price of the soup special?"</span>)
    <span class="pl-en">print</span>(<span class="pl-s1">response</span>.<span class="pl-c1">content</span>)

    <span class="pl-c"># Output:</span>
    <span class="pl-c"># The price of the Clam Chowder, which is the soup special, is $9.99.</span>

<span class="pl-s1">asyncio</span>.<span class="pl-c1">run</span>(<span class="pl-en">main</span>()) </pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Agent with Plugin - .NET</h3><a id="user-content-agent-with-plugin---net" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Agent with Plugin - .NET" href="#agent-with-plugin---net"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-cs notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="using System.ComponentModel;
using Microsoft.SemanticKernel;
using Microsoft.SemanticKernel.Agents;
using Microsoft.SemanticKernel.ChatCompletion;

var builder = Kernel.CreateBuilder();
builder.AddAzureOpenAIChatCompletion(
                Environment.GetEnvironmentVariable(&quot;AZURE_OPENAI_DEPLOYMENT&quot;),
                Environment.GetEnvironmentVariable(&quot;AZURE_OPENAI_ENDPOINT&quot;),
                Environment.GetEnvironmentVariable(&quot;AZURE_OPENAI_API_KEY&quot;)
                );
var kernel = builder.Build();

kernel.Plugins.Add(KernelPluginFactory.CreateFromType&lt;MenuPlugin&gt;());

ChatCompletionAgent agent =
    new()
    {
        Name = &quot;SK-Assistant&quot;,
        Instructions = &quot;You are a helpful assistant.&quot;,
        Kernel = kernel,
        Arguments = new KernelArguments(new PromptExecutionSettings() { FunctionChoiceBehavior = FunctionChoiceBehavior.Auto() })

    };

await foreach (AgentResponseItem&lt;ChatMessageContent&gt; response 
    in agent.InvokeAsync(&quot;What is the price of the soup special?&quot;))
{
    Console.WriteLine(response.Message);
}

        &quot;$9.99&quot;;

<span class="pl-k">sealed</span> <span class="pl-k">class</span> <span class="pl-smi">MenuPlugin</span>
<span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-c1">KernelFunction</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">Description</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">"Provides a list of specials from the menu."</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span>
    <span class="pl-k">public</span> <span class="pl-smi">string</span> <span class="pl-en">GetSpecials</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span>
        <span class="pl-s">"""</span>
<span class="pl-s">        Special Soup: Clam Chowder</span>
<span class="pl-s">        Special Salad: Cobb Salad</span>
<span class="pl-s">        Special Drink: Chai Tea</span>
<span class="pl-s">        """</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

    <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-c1">KernelFunction</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">Description</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">"Provides the price of the requested menu item."</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span>
    <span class="pl-k">public</span> <span class="pl-smi">string</span> <span class="pl-en">GetItemPrice</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span>
        <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-c1">Description</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">"The name of the menu item."</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span>
        <span class="pl-smi">string</span> <span class="pl-s1">menuItem</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span>
        <span class="pl-s">"$9.99"</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Multi-Agent System - Python</h3><a id="user-content-multi-agent-system---python" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Multi-Agent System - Python" href="#multi-agent-system---python"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Build a system of specialized agents that can collaborate:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="import asyncio
from semantic_kernel.agents import ChatCompletionAgent, ChatHistoryAgentThread
from semantic_kernel.connectors.ai.open_ai import AzureChatCompletion, OpenAIChatCompletion

billing_agent = ChatCompletionAgent(
    service=AzureChatCompletion(), 
    name=&quot;BillingAgent&quot;, 
    instructions=&quot;You handle billing issues like charges, payment methods, cycles, fees, discrepancies, and payment failures.&quot;
)

refund_agent = ChatCompletionAgent(
    service=AzureChatCompletion(),
    name=&quot;RefundAgent&quot;,
    instructions=&quot;Assist users with refund inquiries, including eligibility, policies, processing, and status updates.&quot;,
)

triage_agent = ChatCompletionAgent(
    service=OpenAIChatCompletion(),
    name=&quot;TriageAgent&quot;,
    instructions=&quot;Evaluate user requests and forward them to BillingAgent or RefundAgent for targeted assistance.&quot;
    &quot; Provide the full answer to the user containing any information from the agents&quot;,
    plugins=[billing_agent, refund_agent],
)

thread: ChatHistoryAgentThread = None

async def main() -&gt; None:
    print(&quot;Welcome to the chat bot!\n  Type 'exit' to exit.\n  Try to get some billing or refund help.&quot;)
    while True:
        user_input = input(&quot;User:&gt; &quot;)

        if user_input.lower().strip() == &quot;exit&quot;:
            print(&quot;\n\nExiting chat...&quot;)
            return False

        response = await triage_agent.get_response(
            messages=user_input,
            thread=thread,
        )

        if response:
            print(f&quot;Agent :&gt; {response}&quot;)

# Agent :&gt; I understand that you were charged twice for your subscription last month, and I'm here to assist you with resolving this issue. Heres what we need to do next:

# 1. **Billing Inquiry**:
#    - Please provide the email address or account number associated with your subscription, the date(s) of the charges, and the amount charged. This will allow the billing team to investigate the discrepancy in the charges.

# 2. **Refund Process**:
#    - For the refund, please confirm your subscription type and the email address associated with your account.
#    - Provide the dates and transaction IDs for the charges you believe were duplicated.

# Once we have these details, we will be able to:

# - Check your billing history for any discrepancies.
# - Confirm any duplicate charges.
# - Initiate a refund for the duplicate payment if it qualifies. The refund process usually takes 5-10 business days after approval.

# Please provide the necessary details so we can proceed with resolving this issue for you.


if __name__ == &quot;__main__&quot;:
    asyncio.run(main())"><pre><span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">asyncio</span>
<span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s1">semantic_kernel</span>.<span class="pl-s1">agents</span> <span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-v">ChatCompletionAgent</span>, <span class="pl-v">ChatHistoryAgentThread</span>
<span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s1">semantic_kernel</span>.<span class="pl-s1">connectors</span>.<span class="pl-s1">ai</span>.<span class="pl-s1">open_ai</span> <span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-v">AzureChatCompletion</span>, <span class="pl-v">OpenAIChatCompletion</span>

<span class="pl-s1">billing_agent</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">ChatCompletionAgent</span>(
    <span class="pl-s1">service</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-en">AzureChatCompletion</span>(), 
    <span class="pl-s1">name</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"BillingAgent"</span>, 
    <span class="pl-s1">instructions</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"You handle billing issues like charges, payment methods, cycles, fees, discrepancies, and payment failures."</span>
)

<span class="pl-s1">refund_agent</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">ChatCompletionAgent</span>(
    <span class="pl-s1">service</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-en">AzureChatCompletion</span>(),
    <span class="pl-s1">name</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"RefundAgent"</span>,
    <span class="pl-s1">instructions</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"Assist users with refund inquiries, including eligibility, policies, processing, and status updates."</span>,
)

<span class="pl-s1">triage_agent</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">ChatCompletionAgent</span>(
    <span class="pl-s1">service</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-en">OpenAIChatCompletion</span>(),
    <span class="pl-s1">name</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"TriageAgent"</span>,
    <span class="pl-s1">instructions</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"Evaluate user requests and forward them to BillingAgent or RefundAgent for targeted assistance."</span>
    <span class="pl-s">" Provide the full answer to the user containing any information from the agents"</span>,
    <span class="pl-s1">plugins</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span>[<span class="pl-s1">billing_agent</span>, <span class="pl-s1">refund_agent</span>],
)

<span class="pl-s1">thread</span>: <span class="pl-smi">ChatHistoryAgentThread</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">None</span>

<span class="pl-k">async</span> <span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>() <span class="pl-c1">-&gt;</span> <span class="pl-c1">None</span>:
    <span class="pl-en">print</span>(<span class="pl-s">"Welcome to the chat bot!<span class="pl-cce">\n</span>  Type 'exit' to exit.<span class="pl-cce">\n</span>  Try to get some billing or refund help."</span>)
    <span class="pl-k">while</span> <span class="pl-c1">True</span>:
        <span class="pl-s1">user_input</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">input</span>(<span class="pl-s">"User:&gt; "</span>)

        <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-s1">user_input</span>.<span class="pl-c1">lower</span>().<span class="pl-c1">strip</span>() <span class="pl-c1">==</span> <span class="pl-s">"exit"</span>:
            <span class="pl-en">print</span>(<span class="pl-s">"<span class="pl-cce">\n</span><span class="pl-cce">\n</span>Exiting chat..."</span>)
            <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">False</span>

        <span class="pl-s1">response</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">await</span> <span class="pl-s1">triage_agent</span>.<span class="pl-c1">get_response</span>(
            <span class="pl-s1">messages</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s1">user_input</span>,
            <span class="pl-s1">thread</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s1">thread</span>,
        )

        <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-s1">response</span>:
            <span class="pl-en">print</span>(<span class="pl-s">f"Agent :&gt; <span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">response</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>"</span>)

<span class="pl-c"># 1. **Billing Inquiry**:</span>

<span class="pl-c">#    - For the refund, please confirm your subscription type and the email address associated with your account.</span>

<span class="pl-c"># - Check your billing history for any discrepancies.</span>
